IT_US_FATE_TAIYAKI_EXPR Casts Quicken status on user for three turns.
IT_US_FATE_TAIYAKI_FLAVOR A fish-shaped bean jam-filled snack sold at the "Edomae-ya" food stall found in the shopping district. Despite its low price, it's packed with bean jam right to the end of the tail, making it extremely popular among students. The pastry is soft and fluffy, and it's apparently still pretty tasty even when it's cooled down.
IT_US_FATE_SANDWICH_EXPR Removes all statuses except Death Sentence and slightly recovers HP.
IT_US_FATE_SANDWICH_FLAVOR A special sandwich made by Rin Tohsaka. She gets up early in the morning to make them, and they're certainly very special, with a delicious flavor that'll satisfy even the most discerning of gourmands.
IT_UG_APPLE_FATE_EXPR An apple that raises a unit's Exp (extra-large amount).
IT_UG_APPLE_FATE_FLAVOR This apple is said to be imbued with magical energy. This energy is passed onto the user, and lives on forever inside him or her. The apple has the power to improve the owner's fate, and is extremely rare and valuable.
IT_UG_APPLE_PUNK_EXPR An apple that raises a unit's Exp (extra-large amount).
IT_UG_APPLE_PUNK_FLAVOR This apple is said to be imbued with memories of Dulyn's research. These memories are inherited by the user, and live on forever inside him or her. It looks like an apple fairy, but saying this out loud will cause it to become angry and indignant.
IT_UG_APPLE_SHINOBI_EXPR An apple that raises a unit's Exp (extra-large amount).
IT_UG_APPLE_SHINOBI_FLAVOR This apple is said to be imbued with memories of the Land of Shinobi. These memories are inherited by the user, and live on forever inside him or her. It's mechanized, and can move autonomously--caution is advised, as if left unattended it may wander off by itself.
IT_US_DIS_ELIXIR_EXPR Greatly recovers unit's HP & slightly recovers Jewels on next turn
IT_US_DIS_ELIXIR_FLAVOR This item is renowned in the Netherworlds as one of the most effective healing items available: it is able to instantly recover a demon's stamina and energy. Its scarcity makes it highly valuable, but in one Netherworld it is apparently used in large quantities to make curry...
IT_US_DIS_KAMIWAZA_EXPR Lowers enemy unit's PATK/MATK and raises own PATK/MATK when attacking (steals stats)
IT_US_DIS_KAMIWAZA_FLAVOR This glove is thought to be modelled after the hand of a famous Netherworld thief. As its name suggests, its stealing capabilities are truly awesome: it is able to plunder physical and magical attack power from foes and add it to the user's own attack power.
IT_US_FF_CONS_STEW_EXPR Raises PATK & greatly recovers HP
IT_US_FF_CONS_STEW_FLAVOR This stew is packed with vegetables and the meat of a ferocious monster. Its seasoning requires careful attention, and it must be constantly stirred in order to stop it from burning, but the end result is well worth it.

IT_US_SQ_RESIST_MIST_FLAVOR
IT_US_FF_STEAK_EXPR Raises Max HP of the unit (amount of HP gained will be added to your current HP)
IT_US_FF_STEAK_FLAVOR Ignis, who likes to cook, takes time and care in cooking the prime rib made from the meat of Garulessa. A dish that appetizes with the aroma of garlic and sauce, just one bite can rejuvenate anyone in an instant.

IT_US_POTION_EXPR Medicine that recovers a unit's HP (small amount).
IT_US_POTION_FLAVOR This bottle contains an elixir that is said to be able to instantly heal any wound. It is effective on not only humans, but also transmuted Phantoms. Due to its high potency, it is most commonly sold in small bottles of this size.
IT_US_HIGH_POTION_EXPR Medicine that recovers a unit's HP (medium amount).
IT_US_HIGH_POTION_FLAVOR This bottle contains an elixir that is said to be able to instantly heal any wound. It is effective on not only humans, but also transmuted Phantoms. This larger-than-average dose is popular with adventurers embarking on lengthy journeys.
IT_US_EXTRA_POTION_EXPR Medicine that recovers a unit's HP (large amount).
IT_US_EXTRA_POTION_FLAVOR This bottle contains an elixir that is said to be able to instantly heal any wound. It is effective on not only humans, but also transmuted Phantoms. This large bottle is quite pricey, but when traveling in dangerous areas a dose of this size could well prove to be a lifesaver.
IT_US_PANACEA_EXPR Medicine that removes all statuses except Death Sentence.
IT_US_PANACEA_FLAVOR This beautiful, rainbow-colored potion is made from a mix of several different elixirs. It lives up to its name, and is able to simultaneously cure a range of different ailments. Its taste, however, is quite unpalatable. It was first concocted by chance long ago, but its effectiveness means it is still a best seller to this day.
IT_US_POISON_EXPR Medicine that removes Poison status.
IT_US_POISON_FLAVOR This elixir has been mixed with special ingredients extracted from a variety of sources, such as crystals and berries, imbuing it with additional properties. It will relieve Poison status, and despite its off-putting appearance, in fact has a pleasant, sweet flavor.
IT_US_ENERGY_EXPR Medicine that removes Daze, Silence, and Bind statuses.
IT_US_ENERGY_FLAVOR This elixir has been mixed with special ingredients extracted from a variety of sources, such as crystals and berries, imbuing it with additional properties. It will relieve Daze, Silence, and Bind statuses. Its striking green hue is reminiscent of young leaves, and it tastes like fresh grass.
IT_US_VITALITY_EXPR Medicine that removes stat reductions.
IT_US_VITALITY_FLAVOR This elixir has been mixed with special ingredients extracted from a variety of sources, such as crystals and berries, imbuing it with additional properties. It will relieve stat reductions. It has an extremely spicy flavor that is at odds with its pastel pink hue.
IT_US_LIFE_EXPR Medicine that removes Death Sentence status.
IT_US_LIFE_FLAVOR Designed with an angelic motif, this bell emits a beautiful, gentle tone when rung. It was originally made in an area of Lustburg and sold as a protective amulet. The sound it makes is said to steer the bearer away from death.
IT_US_POWDER_POWER_EXPR Powder that raises PATK/MATK.
IT_US_POWDER_POWER_FLAVOR Made by extracting Alchemia from plants, this powder grants temporary enhancements to the body. The dosage size required varies depending on the type of powder, but each one has the same herb-like taste. This green powder only requires a small dose to work, and is able to activate dormant power within the body.

IT_US_POWDER_GUARD_FLAVOR Made by extracting Alchemia from plants, this powder grants temporary enhancements to the body. The dosage size required varies depending on the type of powder, but each one has the same herb-like taste. This orange powder requires a fairly large dose to have any effect, but is able to boost the body's defensive properties.

IT_US_POWDER_HP_FLAVOR Made by extracting Alchemia from plants, this powder grants temporary enhancements to the body. This yellow powder requires the largest dose of all the different types, but is able to amplify the user's stamina.

IT_KEY_QUEST_POK_SAM_FLAVOR This key can only be obtained by those who have traversed each of the three worlds. It allows the bearer to travel past the Door of Truth, to the land where the three worlds meet, and be granted any one wish.
IT_KEY_QUEST_3TITLE_SUN_EXPR Using this item at the Key Quest menu will unlock The Sun God and the Golden Key.
IT_KEY_QUEST_3TITLE_SUN_FLAVOR This sacred key is able to control and manipulate the power of the sun. It is also known as the "Golden Key," and its purpose is to save the shining sun and its guardian. It is imbued with a powerful energy, and the key itself is dazzling to behold.

IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_2_EXPR This item can be used to evolve a piece of 2★ gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_2_FLAVOR This Alchemia-rich ore boasts good affinity with commonly available gear. It can be used to evolve a piece of gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_3_EXPR This item can be used to evolve a piece of 3★ gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_3_FLAVOR This Alchemia-rich ore boasts good affinity with gear of medium-level availability. It can be used to evolve a piece of gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_4_EXPR This item can be used to evolve a piece of 4★ gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_RARE_4_FLAVOR This Alchemia-rich ore boasts good affinity with very rare and valuable gear. It can be used to evolve a piece of gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
IT_AF_COMMON_ALL_FLAVOR This all-purpose, Alchemia-rich ore boasts good affinity with any and all gear. It can be used to evolve a piece of gear in place of that piece of gear's corresponding Gear Shard.
